
JMdict  - Additional 外来語 Readings
Below is a collection of 外来語 entries (in EDICT2 format) which are
mostly either compound nouns or multiword expressions. Each has with it
or more proposed additional versions with interpunct (中黒/・) characters
marking the word segmentation.
The segmentation has been done automatically using the 
system available at this
server. 
There are about 9,100 entries, and about 9,400 extra readings. The segmentation was not always accurate,
so I went through them and amended/removed a lot that looked wrong/odd.
Please let me know if you see any (more) errors.
Jim Breen
April/May 2013
